<h2>All Reviews</h2>

<ol>
    <li> This is the best BB cream I&#x27;ve ever used, hands down, and I&#x27;ve tried close to 20, mostly Asian but some European and American brands too. This feels like a \\&quot;second skin\\&quot; and it oxidizes to perfectly match, blend, and \\&quot;brighten\\&quot; my skin tone. With other foundations and BB creams I always felt like I was wearing something, but this just melds with my skin. I cannot think of one thing to complain about. I love the packaging even!</li>
    <li> I had purchased sample bb creams before to choose the right bb cream for me, when i got this i saw that it was a small size but still i was happy to have received it, for some reason the consistency was not the same as i had remembered but it was still ok, it was a bit runny, and left me looking a bit too dewy but it was somewhat the same as other bb creams i had tried. Will keep on looking for other products but will maybe purchase this in the near future.</li>
    <li> Great coverage, doesn&#x27;t feel oily. Will keep purchasing over and over again. I am now using this instead of traditional foundation!</li>
    <li> American cosmetics companies have gotten into the BB cream business lately, but the ones I&#x27;ve tried from Garnier and L&#x27;Oreal are just basically tinted moisturizer. But this cream is thick, and unlike American products has a greyish tint to it. That sounds awful, I know, but I have pale skin, freckles and some red splotchiness around my nose and chin when I get out of the shower, and this smoothes everything over and looks great after it&#x27;s absorbed. I used to moisturize and then add foundation and powder, now I just use this right out of the shower, no makeup sponge necessary, and brush a little powder on top. And compared to department-store foundations this is a teriffic bargain.</li>
    <li> Few months ago, after all the hype about BB creams, I bought Missha Perfect BB Cream #23, Etude House Precious Mineral BB Cream #13, and Skin 79 pink label BB Cream (Ebay seller in Korea).  Also bought Smash Box BB cream and tried many other American brands BB creams (Dior, Boscia, Too Face, Tarte).  I have combination, normal to oil skin, thus, make-up only lasts about 4 hours, even though I work indoor (I am a once-a-day make-up kindda girl). B/c of popularity of Missha, I used it first.  Some reasons, I felt it was too heavy, too oily.  Then I switched to Skin 79 and Etude House.  They all go on every smooth and easy to blend (I use stippling brush).  Skin 79 pink label only comes in 1 color and it&#x27;s sheer/light coverage.  It&#x27;s even out my skin but it does not cover capillary red spots or black spots due to acnes.  It lasts 4-5 hours.  Etude House Precious Mineral #13 is a bit light for me.  It is medium coverage.  However, I found that it&#x27;s a bit dry.  It makes me flaky around the nose area.  I decided to use Etude House as concealer.  Not the best but it works.  It also works when I mix Skin 79 and Etude House together.  Neither one of these products have any fragant to it.  Missha BB cream does have fragrant.  It smells like baby powder-ish.  It&#x27;s not bad (it eventually goes away after after few hours); however, I really don&#x27;t care for the smell.  Some people actually like the fragrant (on youtube). That was also one other reason I stopped using Missha.  After months, I decided to \\&quot;re-visit\\&quot; Missha BB cream again.  Still don&#x27;t care for the fragrant; however, it gives a medium coverage.  My skin is very clear except for the capillary red spots around the nose and occasional black acne spots.  So I don&#x27;t really need a \\&quot;heavy\\&quot; coverage (I used Laura Bare Mineral and Mercier tinted moisturizure for a long time).  However, with a bit of setting powder, Missha BB cream lasts almost all day.  Plus of Missha BB cream, high SPF (maybe that why it seems more oily).&lt;br /&gt;In summary, for medium coverage Missha (if you don&#x27;t mind the fragrant), Etude House (if you don&#x27;t have dry skin).  For light coverage, Skin 79.  Tips: even though, BB creams are all in one products, always wear moisturizures (&#x3D;/- additional sun block) and setting powder.  Even though, you can build for more coverage, but I&#x27;d not recommended b/c it will look very heavy.  Also, buy from a reputable Ebay sellers.  It is cheaper than amazon, around $11-13.  Beware, fake products are out there (I do not understand this either b/c it&#x27;s not every expensive, why do people make/sell fake products).  I suspect that these products are \\&quot;drug-store\\&quot; brands in Korea.  But since we can&#x27;t get our hands on, we are paying a bit more.  Next, I want to try Tony Molly CC cream.&lt;br /&gt;As for American brands, Smash Box is heavy, almost like foundation.  Dior BB creams are more of yellow tone and dark.  Tarte is too powdery for my liking.  Boscia is water base so it&#x27;s nice; however, it&#x27;s one shade and not recommended for darker than NC-35.  Too Face gives a dewy/sheer/natural look and good for yellow tone skin.&lt;br /&gt;Hope you will find a right products.</li>
    <li> Love it. I have oily skin and this bb cream does not make it more oily, it covers great an feels great on skin.</li>
    <li> This is FAKE and gave me awful breakout!!! The first day using it was fine, actually good coverage, but starting from the second day breakout came!</li>

Do yourself a favor and spend your money instead on Face Shop BB Cream: http://www.amazon.com/THE-FACE-SHOP-Magic-Natural/dp/B0054U56GO/. This one&#x27;s lasted me almost a year and still going strong, full, weightless coverage, and you use less of it.</li>
    <li> My complexion isn&#x27;t really that light or dark for a Mexican, but the cream blends in really nicely and gets rid of the small blemishes I have from sun exposure, acne, etc. The best thing about is that it makes my skin look really smooth and natural since the cream is really light so it&#x27;s actually like, the perfect product for me since I don&#x27;t like wearing makeup anyways (the most I use is some mascara and a small thin layer of eyeliner.)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;So if you&#x27;re looking for something to just smooth/even out your face, this shit&#x27;s the way to go.</li>
    <li> I have tried a few BB creams but certainly not all.  This one is on the thicker side so it provides a bit more coverage than some.  I wish they had more colors.  I found this to be on the gray side, almost ashy in color.</li>
    <li> This cream is exactly what I have always needed for my skin, and at 27 years old, I have finally found it.  My skin is very fair/light and acne prone.  My skintone is a little uneven and is combination.  I use almost one full pump of BB cream on my face to start with, and it does an amazing job of evening my skintone out and giving it a nice, dewy glow.  Then, I use some concealer under my eyes and finish up with MAC loose powder in light.  I can tell a huge difference in my face, my acne has greatly improved and my makeup has never looked better.  I highly recommend this product, I have tried dozens of low-end and high-end creams, powders, treatments, masks, foundations, mousse, you name it, and this BB cream is the best thing that has ever happened to my face!</li>

    <li> I work outdoors, and I like simplicity, so I was looking for a single face product that has good spf, decent coverage, and would not wear off from sweat or rain. I had an amazon gift card, and used part of it on a mini set of Skin 79.  The &amp;#34;hot pink&amp;#34; was my favorite out of that bunch.  The first day I wore it, I went to spinning class - I thought it was a perfect test for the durability and sweat-proof-ness.  75 minutes later, I am astonished to say that this product (mostly) stayed put!!!  Wha?!?  I thought, &amp;#34;Since it lasted through spin, it must be excessively harsh, so I will be breaking out any minute now.&amp;#34;  Well, that never happened either.     <li> I love this BB cream and wear it just about every day. I&#x27;ve tried samples of American BB creams from Sephora, and this one is better than all of them. It looks a little yellow or grayish right out of the bottle, but once I rub it in it blends in perfectly with my alabaster skin tone. It evens out any redness and makes it look like I have perfect skin without makeup. It gives me a slightly dewy look, and I brush on a little Bare Minerals powder if I want a matte finish.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The only reason I&#x27;m giving it 4 stars instead of 5 is that the pump container means you have know idea how much product is left. One day I pump it and it&#x27;s fine, the next day it&#x27;s out. There&#x27;s no way to remove the top and scrape out the remaining BB cream. If it were in a tube or jar I could tell how much was left and also be sure I got every last bit out of it.</li>
    <li> This cream has a light coverage but evens my skin tone and does not irritate or make my sensitive skin break out :)</li>
    <li> I love everything about this product... except that I&#x27;m allergic to it! It goes on very nourishing and moisturizing at first, gives great coverage, and blends easily to match my pale skin. It looks flawless. However, after using this product every day for 1 week, I noticed that after a few hours, my skin started feeling very tight. By the end of the day, my forehead was flaking. I use moisturizer before applying this product though. In fact, I have not changed anything about my skin care routine except for adding this BB cream. I also now have small hives all over my face. At first I thought it was acne, but the spots are coming in places where I don&#x27;t normally breakout. I have never had acne on my cheeks or eyelids... ever! But now I have these little red spots that are itchy and dry. This is very unfortunate because this was so close to being my favorite product and replacing foundation forever. I have not heard of anyone else having this problem though. I would definitely give the product a try, but beware! I really don&#x27;t have sensitive skin, but I do get eczema occasionally on my body. I have never had it on my face and I think this product has caused that. Just something to think about...</li>

This BB not only gives you great coverage but makes your skin almost glow, it helps to keep my oily face nice and dry and my other makeup just falls into place and stays there. Now, yes it does have a grey ash color but as you blend it in the BB will match your color, a little goes a long way so use about 5 small pumps and spread evenly with a concealer brush.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;*UPDATE* 10/10/2012&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Ok. So I thought it fair to update my review since there&#x27;s some issues that can change your mind. I am sad to report that I am returning both of my BB creams to the seller because I feel that I bought fakes. I was developing a rash so I started eliminating products until finally I had to admit it was the BB cream. I sought out information online on how to spot a fake and I found that there are a lot of contradictions. The ones I bought seem to be ok, however the BB on one of them has completely rubbed off and the other one is slowly fading. I am not sure if is because is a fake or because it&#x27;s out in the open. To be sure I went to the Skin79 website where they only provide you with one sure way of verifying authenticity which is to check the silver sticker on the back of your bottle. If you go to their website it will show you the difference between an original sticker and a tampered one. At first glance mines seem to be ok, but if you place it under the light it does look like the tampered image they show you. I have decided to buy the BB cream straight from the Skin79 website just to be sure, it&#x27;s a little more but I rather pay more and have a piece of mind than be cheap and pay for it with my face. Good luck!!</li>

The thing though, about these photos are that Skin79 changes their packages regularly, probably to fool the people who are making fakes out there. The front label on the box and on the bottle says \\&quot;Wrinkle Improvement\\&quot; instead of Wrinkle Free. That freaked me out, because some of the &#x27;Real&#x27; versions out there shows Wrinkle Free. Upon further studying and research, I found out that Skin79 recently changed their products to say Wrinkle Improvement, so +1 there. To all of you who just bought one recently and your bottle still says Wrinkle Free, :&#x27;( idk, check the date if it&#x27;s 2012, should say Wrinkle Improvement! Also as a side note, those who say \\&quot;oh, your product is fake if the labeled words scratch off,\\&quot; that&#x27;s just silly. Almost anything can be scratched off if it&#x27;s out in heat, or dry areas long enough. I also found comments of a person who talked to a representative of cute and pretty, who sells authentic skin79 products, who even said that the label can scratch off, real or fake, if it&#x27;s been let out in the sun or in different conditions long enough. So I think I&#x27;m going to skip that test, haha... not going to sit here and try to scratch off my brand new product to base if it&#x27;s real or not.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Second, the barcode should be on the bottom of the box; mine was on both products, as well as the expiration date and the manufacturing date. The manufacturing date was very recent as well, sometime this year, and expiration date in 2014. On the bottle itself there was also a sticker of authenticity, the gold version wasn&#x27;t as nicely placed as the pink bottle.. it was slightly crooked, which made me worried. Perforated lines on both boxes were shown as well.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Third, If you read inside the box, on the English part I found a typo: it said Wriinkle Improvement. I was like, damn, this is a fake. HOWEVER, after some research I found a lady who bought it full price from a local authorized retailer, and the real product also has this typo, which made me extremely relieved.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Fourth, as a last check, I pumped a little on my hand. I&#x27;ve read that if it comes out leaky or watery, it&#x27;s fake. It came out finely mixed, in one unison color and was lightly fragrant. The pink took like literally 20+ pumps to get it going, and the white only 1 or 2 pumps.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;After all this, I am almost sure now that the product I got was an authentic skin79 product. If you&#x27;ve kept up with me so far, hooray! You are now more informed! These are the elaborate reasons why I think my product is legit. I&#x27;ll be buying from her from now on, unless someone finds new information to prove me wrong.</li>

All and all, I was an extremely happy camper.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Some things to consider: I&#x27;m not incredibly pale, but I am pale enough that this BB cream matched perfectly with my skin, so someone that&#x27;s darker complected or has an olive tone might want to try some of the others that are tinted differently. I smoked for 12 years before quitting 2 years ago and have tiny fine lines under my eyes. Other than that the only wrinkles I have are expression lines on my forehead.&lt;br /&gt;4. I have oily, acne prone skin, though I keep it in check with Duac and Retin-A micro.&lt;br /&gt;5. I tend towards having sensitive skin.&lt;br /&gt;7. I am extremely diligent about washing my face every morning and night, completely removing all traces of makeup.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The reason I outlined all of that for you is because it is important to take note that this product WILL NOT fit every skin type and tone, and it is not intended to. It is designed for Asian skin, and in most eastern cultures having fair, untanned skin is highly desirable, unlike western cultures where everyone spray tans to death.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;That being said, this product applies like a dream: creamy, balmy, but not greasy. At first appearance it may appear to have a gray-ish cast, but that quickly dissipates after being blended into skin. I do not use this as a moisturizer, but instead use my Cera Ve a few minute before applying and allow that to absorb before applying this. This evens my skin tone out perfectly, although I do need to use a little concealer under my dark circles.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To my fourth point above, I do have oily skin, and this product is designed to control oil. I set it with Maybelline Shine Free loose powder and have noticed a substantial decrease in the oiliness and shine of my skin.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Now, onto my biggest rave of this product. In addition to leaving my skin flawless and beautiful while I&#x27;m wearing it, my skin is actually improving after I take it off! I started noticing this effect after about 2 weeks of using the product almost daily. I did not anticipate this effect; indeed, it is what inspired me to write this review. The expression lines on my forehead are actually noticeably diminished, my pores appear tighter, and my skin is baby soft and smooth. Now, I do use Retin A micro and I exfoliate a few times a week with a polishing brush, but I have never noticed this kind of effect with any other cosmetic product. I have an overall glow and any little marks that I had due to old acne are disappearing too. I attribute that to the whitening agent in this and the face that there are so many natural ingredients.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;A little side note-BB cream was actually developed to help plastic surgery patients heal post-opt. It allowed them to blend their scars away while healing. That should tell you something.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Sorry for the long review, but I felt it was important to point out that this product can and does work miracles for the right kind of skin type and tone. If you have extremely dry skin, this may not work for you. Skin 79 offers different formulas that are designed for different skin types; you can check their website for more detailed information. If you have olive or tan skin, or plan to use tanning beds/go out in the sun/spray tan, this is not the right thing for you. Also, if you are not diligent about your skin and do not wash it off at night, I do not think you would get the same effects I have. It really is a cosmetic and needs to be applied to clean skin in the morning and removed at night. I suspect that it would be easy to think of this as a lotion and not bother washing it off.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Overall, I truly love this product and can&#x27;t wait to explore other Skin 79 products.     <li> This BB cream is the best I&#x27;ve tried as far as texture and coverage without feeling heavy, and believe me when I say I&#x27;ve tried A LOT of BB creams. Barely any scent at all either, which I love. It feels like I have nothing on my face, which is exactly the feel I&#x27;m going for. My skin is super oily with big pores in the t-zone and this is fantastic in covering those imperfections and in keeping the shine at bay. Like I&#x27;ve said, I have tried many other BB creams, even ones made for oily skin, but nothing has made my skin feel good like this one. I&#x27;m not dark skinned at all. I&#x27;m actually Asian with light/medium skin tone. However, this makes me look very pale wearing it, like I haven&#x27;t seen the sun in forever. I really wish they made one a shade darker, and it would be a perfect product!</li>
    <li> So when I first heard about BB Creams, they sounded exactly like what I needed. I tried a few washed-down American BB creams and liked the moisturizer and sunscreen, but the coverage was just not enough for daily wear. So then I tried Skin79&#x27;s BB cream. I figured I could use it on my &amp;#34;light&amp;#34; makeup days and wear my typical foundation on the regular days. After using it, I haven&#x27;t even touched my traditional foundations again.     <li> I&#x27;ve used both Missha and Skin79, and I thought I&#x27;d wait until I finished both products to write my review. I&#x27;ll probably break it open to make sure I can use the rest of it. My skin looks really nice, no wrinkles, and I rarely break out. I wear it under loose powder, which helps set the product and make it last longer throughout the day. Both BB Creams look weird when you first put it on, but eventually blends to your skin tone.     <li> I can&#x27;t believe I wasted so much money on American BB creams! The coverage is medium but it&#x27;s still really lightweight. So far no breakouts.     <li> First of all, just a warning that this review will be lengthy, but it comes from the heart and speaks the truth on my part, and this is the kind of review I was looking for before purchasing this product because I hate purchasing new, expensive make up that I take a risk on and then hate and never use again, so hopefully it helps you! ;) If it&#x27;s too long for you, just know that I LOVE it and that&#x27;s all you need to know -- you won&#x27;t be disappointed. :) But if you want more details, read further!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I just want everyone to take heed: *this bb cream is NOTHING like American bb creams -- and I mean that in the best possible way ever*, so *do not* judge Korean bb creams off of American ones. American bb creams are more like a tinted moisturizer, while Korean bb creams are a magical make up wonder.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To give you a little background, I am a 22-year-old, my skin is combination, I suffer from moderate acne especially in my T zone and especially when I am hormonal. My skin is light, and depending on how much sun I&#x27;ve gotten can range from an ivory to a light nude color. I have freckles. I have dark under eye circles and some scars on my skin from past acne. I wear make up almost every day that I have to socially interact with the world (well, maybe not every day, because a girl&#x27;s gotta let her skin breathe and get&#x27;s a little lazy...) even if it&#x27;s just foundation of some type and mascara, and I always hope my makeup lasts all day, with anywhere from working at my internship at a desk job rubbing my eyes and squeezing my head from stress or working outside in my yard or going for a walk with my dog later in the day.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have *always* worn foundation since I started wearing makeup around 8th grade. I really wanted it to even out my tone and cover blemishes. One problem that I have with foundation is that it is SO thick and it easily transfers to other things. It always looks so amazing when you first put it on, but wait a few hours, do a few things, and you&#x27;ll notice considerable deterioration of the look of your make up. I&#x27;ve tried so many different kinds, from expensive Clinique to cheap E.L.F. For those of you who know my tale of woe, you know what I&#x27;m talking about. For those of you who don&#x27;t, foundation easily covers up my freckles, and the second you put your hand on your face and touch a doorknob or keyboard later in the day, there&#x27;s a good chance that some of your makeup will transfer to your hands and other things. For good coverage, the amount of foundation you&#x27;ll need (and keep needing, if you need to keep applying it throughout the day to cover imperfections) can be massive. I never considered that there would be something that works like a foundation but doesn&#x27;t cause all those other problems. That sounded too good to be true. :)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To give you a little background on how I came across this product, I&#x27;ll tell you a quick story. I actually was on the interstate on my way to work when my car broke down. I was horrified, having to get my car towed standing in dress clothes and heels looking like a fool as everyone passed me. I thought it was the worst day ever. But when I got into the car with the man who towed my car, his wife was waiting in the truck, too. She was from South Korea and was the sweetest thing ever and instantly made my day brighter. I told her that I was a big fan of South Korea&#x27;s fashion scene, and she rummaged in her purse and gave me a little tube of make up. She told me everyone in South Korea loves bb cream (authentic Korean, not American, bb cream) and swears by it. The kind of bb cream was Charm Cell and it looked goofy but I thanked her regardless. It was nice.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The next day, I got up and took a peek at it, not sure if I should put anything on my face from a stranger. I opened it and it was sealed, and then I looked up online more information about the product. My jaw dropped when I saw it retailed to 70 DOLLARS for a small tube! I tried it out for the next weekand fell in love. I&#x27;ll tell you my revelations on why below, so keep reading. I didn&#x27;t end up wanting to spend 70 dollars for a small tube, so I researched other top brands, and Skin79 was one of them. I&#x27;m so happy I went down this route.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;First of all, I have to say that my skin is BETTER than it ever has been before after using Skin79&#x27;s Hot Pink bb cream. I&#x27;ve never actually worn make up that I believe improves my complexion, allows me to have my *natural* skin but still covers blemishes, and feels light weight and fresh. I purposely waited A MONTH to write this review so that I didn&#x27;t just rant or rave after a day, or even a week after trying this product. You have to give it a little time, too to see any long term results, whether good or bad for you.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Some of the major things I&#x27;ve noticed: My acne has decreased. My skin tone has evened (not as much of a drastic difference between a face with no make up vs. a face with make up). my make up breathes better and isn&#x27;t completely obvious that I&#x27;m wearing it on my face (you know, the whole \\&quot;it makes you look more professional and naturally pretty instead of obviously fake pancake face\\&quot;). You can still see my freckles (depending on whether you&#x27;re proud to don those or not, and if not, use a little of your foundation on top to cover them, this bb cream works great as a primer :)) It blends PERFECTLY into my face. It smells nice and doesn&#x27;t leave residue everywhere. It LASTS for almost the whole day and looks great!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;A few tips: don&#x27;t just pump a large amount into your hand and rub your face. Start small and use a small amount. There&#x27;s a certain technique to putting it on that you can read about online (I hope to post a review/tutorial soon to my own website, so I&#x27;ll update this review when I do). Just dab small dots all over your face and then *pat* it into your skin, don&#x27;t rub. Apply two to three applications depending on how much coverage you want.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;A lot of people mention a greyish tone when it first goes on, but I don&#x27;t find this with mine. I feel like if you put on just enough and not too much, you won&#x27;t run into that problem.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;On days when I want a bit more coverage and to look more flawless on my face (say, for a special occasion) I take my regular foundation (I use E.L.F. liquid foundation, that&#x27;s amazing too, you should check it out) and just apply a little bit around my under eye circles and around my mouth and jawline. It blends in PERFECTLY with the bb cream and I find it sets better with the BB cream acting as a primer as well (assuming you give the bb cream a few minutes to dry before you apply the foundation). I also use a bronzer or matting powder to set the bb cream and I find this makes it stay even better.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;All in all, I COMPLETELY recommend this. I&#x27;m your average girl who tried this after a chance encounter and a lot of reading of reviews online, and I am telling you that I&#x27;m impressed. I would hope this product would work as well for all of you, but realistically I know that not all make up is created equal for each person.
